## 🎓 TEACHING RULES — HOW TO EXPLAIN THINGS

These rules are **non-negotiable**. Every code response MUST follow them.

### Rule T1 — Explain Before Code
Before showing ANY new Kotlin/Python/Bash code that uses a concept the developer hasn't seen before:
- Write a plain-English explanation (2-4 sentences) of WHAT the concept is
- Write a simple real-life analogy (e.g., "Hilt is like a restaurant kitchen that prepares ingredients before a chef needs them — so the chef (ViewModel) doesn't have to go shopping himself")
- THEN show the code

### Rule T2 — Line-by-Line Comments (MANDATORY)
**Every single line of code you write MUST have a comment explaining what it does.**
This rule applies to:
- Kotlin Android code
- Python server/scraping code
- Bash/shell scripts
- Docker Compose YAML
- Gradle build files
- XML files (if any)
- JSON config files

**Comment style:**
```kotlin
// ✅ CORRECT — beginner-friendly comment style
val micButton = remember { mutableStateOf(false) }
// ^ 'remember' keeps this value alive across Compose redraws (like a sticky note on the screen)
// ^ 'mutableStateOf(false)' creates a true/false value that starts as 'false' (mic is OFF)
// ^ When this value changes, Jetpack Compose automatically redraws the mic button
```

```python
# ✅ CORRECT — Python comment style
qdrant_client = QdrantClient(host="localhost", port=6333)
# ^ QdrantClient is the Python library that lets us talk to the Qdrant vector database
# ^ host="localhost" means Qdrant is running on the same machine as this Python script
# ^ port=6333 is the door number (port) that Qdrant listens on — like a phone extension
```

```yaml
# ✅ CORRECT — Docker Compose comment style
services:          # 'services' lists all the programs (containers) we want to run
  fastapi:         # This is our main Python web server — handles all Android app requests
    image: python:3.11-slim   # Use Python 3.11 slim (small) Docker image as the base
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"  # Map port 8000 on Ubuntu to port 8000 inside the container
                     # Format: "HOST_PORT:CONTAINER_PORT"
                     # Android app sends requests to Ubuntu:8000 → reaches FastAPI inside Docker
```

### Rule T3 — Teach File Placement
Whenever you create a new file, always state:
- What folder it goes in
- Why it goes there
- How it relates to other files already created

Example:
```
📁 File: app/src/main/java/com/rushdululilm/app/ui/screens/HomeScreen.kt
   Why here: Android Studio looks for UI screens in the 'ui/screens/' folder by convention.
             'com.rushdululilm.app' matches the package name we set in build.gradle.
   Relates to: MainActivity.kt (which calls this screen), NavGraph.kt (which routes to it)
```

### Rule T4 — Show the Full Picture First
Before writing code for any new feature:
1. Show a simple diagram (ASCII or text) of how the feature connects to other parts
2. List ALL files that will be created or modified
3. Estimate how long it will take to understand and implement
4. Then write the code file by file, top to bottom

## 🚫 ANTI-HALLUCINATION RULES — ABSOLUTE PROHIBITIONS

These rules exist to protect the integrity of Islamic knowledge and the developer's time.

### Rule AH1 — NEVER Invent Islamic Rulings
```
❌ STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: Writing or suggesting any Islamic fatwa, ruling, hadith reference,
   or Quranic interpretation from your own LLM knowledge.

✅ CORRECT BEHAVIOUR: Every Islamic answer in app code must come from the RAG pipeline.
   The RAG prompt MUST always include:
   "Answer ONLY from the provided context. Do NOT use your own knowledge.
    If the answer is not in the provided context, say: 'I could not find an answer
    in the approved Islamic sources. Please consult a qualified scholar.'
    Always cite the exact source URL at the end of your answer."
```

### Rule AH2 — NEVER Hallucinate Library Versions or APIs
```
❌ FORBIDDEN: Making up function names, parameters, or API methods for libraries.
✅ REQUIRED: If unsure about an exact API, say:
   "I am not 100% certain of this API signature. Please verify this in the official docs at [URL]."
   Then show the APPROXIMATE code with a comment: // ⚠️ VERIFY THIS API IN DOCS BEFORE RUNNING
```

### Rule AH3 — NEVER Skip the Three-Tier Offline Fallback
```
❌ FORBIDDEN: Implementing any feature that only works with internet — no offline fallback.
✅ REQUIRED: Every feature that needs the internet MUST have all three tiers:
   Tier 1 → Internet (server via cloud/VPS)
   Tier 2 → LAN (server via local Wi-Fi 192.168.x.x)
   Tier 3 → Fully offline (on-device — Room DB, whisper.cpp JNI, Opus-MT ONNX, Android TTS)
```

### Rule AH4 — NEVER Exceed Hardware Limits
```
Developer's GPU: NVIDIA GTX 1650ti — 4GB VRAM ONLY
❌ FORBIDDEN: Suggesting any AI model that needs more than 3.5GB VRAM
✅ ALLOWED models (verified to fit in 4GB VRAM):
   - Qwen3:4b Q4_K_M (2.5GB VRAM) — LLM
   - faster-whisper-large-v3-turbo INT8 (1.5GB VRAM) — STT
   - paraphrase-multilingual-mpnet-base-v2 (CPU, ~420MB RAM) — embeddings
   - IndicTrans2 indic-en-1B (fits in 3GB VRAM with INT8) — translation
   - Coqui XTTS-v2 (fits in 3GB VRAM) — TTS
   If multiple GPU services run together → warn developer to start them one at a time.
```

### Rule AH5 — NEVER Add Telemetry or Third-Party Analytics
```
❌ STRICTLY FORBIDDEN: Adding any of these to the Android app or backend:
   - Google Analytics / Firebase Analytics
   - Google Crashlytics
   - Facebook SDK
   - Any third-party crash reporter or event tracker
   - Any cloud LLM API calls (OpenAI, Anthropic API, Google Gemini API) — ALL inference is local

✅ ONLY ALLOWED tracking: Local app usage stats stored in Room DB on the user's phone only.
```

### Rule AH6 — NEVER Change the Package Name
```
Android package name is fixed: com.rushdululilm.app
❌ FORBIDDEN: Suggesting any other package name — this breaks Play Store listing.
```

### Rule AH7 — Source URL is MANDATORY in Every Answer
```
❌ FORBIDDEN: Showing a fatwa answer in the app without the source URL.
✅ REQUIRED: Every answer displayed must show:
   - The answer text (in user's language)
   - "Source: [clickable URL]" below the answer
   - If multiple sources: list all of them
```

## 🏗️ PROJECT ARCHITECTURE QUICK REFERENCE

```
App Name:        Rushd-ul-Ilm (رشد العلم — Growth of Knowledge)
Package:         com.rushdululilm.app
Language:        Kotlin 2.x (Android) + Python 3.11 (backend)
Android UI:      Jetpack Compose (NO XML layouts)
Architecture:    MVVM + StateFlow + Hilt DI
Local DB:        Room (SQLite wrapper) with FTS5 for offline search
HTTP:            Retrofit + OkHttp → FastAPI server
Video:           ExoPlayer / Media3
Audio capture:   AudioRecord API at 16kHz mono PCM
Offline STT:     whisper.cpp via Android NDK + JNI (ggml-small-q5_0, 182MB)
Offline Trans:   Opus-MT ONNX INT8 via ONNX Runtime Android (~525MB total)
Offline TTS:     Android TextToSpeech API + Google Telugu/Urdu voice packs
Network check:   ConnectivityManager + OkHttp socket ping (200ms timeout)

Server (Ubuntu — GTX 1650ti):
  FastAPI:        port 8000  — main API server
  Ollama:         port 11434 — serves Qwen3:4b Q4_K_M locally
  Qdrant:         port 6333  — vector DB for semantic search
  IndicTrans2:    port 8001  — Telugu/Urdu ↔ English translation
  Coqui XTTS-v2: port 8002  — TTS in Telugu, Urdu, Arabic, English
  faster-whisper: port 8003  — GPU speech-to-text
  Neo4j (Graphiti): ports 7474/7687 — knowledge graph memory
  Mem0:           port 8100  — cross-session agent memory

Islamic Sources (APPROVED — do not add others without developer permission):
  1. https://islamqa.info/en      (Neutral — no madhab)
  2. https://islamqa.org          (Neutral — no madhab)
  3. https://darulifta-deoband.com/en  (Hanafi madhab)
  4. Custom sources (PDFs, Obsidian .md, offline HTML — user-configurable)

Offline data paths on developer's Ubuntu machine:
  islamqa.info:  /home/hidayat/Documents/Islamic Knowledge Q&A App/islamqa.info-offline/
  deoband:       /home/hidayat/Documents/Islamic Knowledge Q&A App/darulifta-deoband.com-offline/
  Videos:        /home/hidayat/Documents/Islamic YouTube Video Database/

Developer machine OS: Parrot OS Linux (primary), Windows (secondary, dual-boot)
```

---

## 📱 UI/UX RULES FOR ILLITERATE USERS — NEVER VIOLATE THESE

```
1. Mic button MUST cover at least 40% of the home screen height — it is the primary action
2. All button labels in BOTH Telugu AND English — never English only
3. Minimum touch target: 48dp for ALL interactive elements
4. Minimum font size: 16sp for ALL user-facing text — never smaller
5. Color coding:
   - Green (#2E7D32) → Islamic/Halal answers, positive guidance
   - Calm blue (#1565C0) → Quranic references
   - Orange (#E65100) → Offline mode indicator (always visible when no internet)
   - Red (#B71C1C) → Errors only
6. 'Read Aloud' button MUST always be visible on answer screen — NEVER hidden in a menu
7. Offline mode MUST show a banner: "📵 Offline Mode — Using Downloaded Knowledge"
8. Answer text in user's language (Telugu/Urdu) is ALWAYS larger than source URL text
9. Loading indicators: always show a spinner with text like "Searching Islamic sources..."
10. No technical error messages to the user — translate them:
    e.g., "HTTP 503" → "Server is busy. Please try again in a moment."
```

## 🧠 MEMORY SYSTEM RULES (Graphiti + Mem0)

When Graphiti and Mem0 are running (see knowledge-graph/ folder for setup):

**At session START:**
```python
# Query Mem0 for last session context
memories = mem0_client.search("Rushd-ul-Ilm current phase task")
# Query Graphiti for project state
result = graphiti_client.search("current development phase files changed")
```

**At session END:**
```python
# Save to Mem0
mem0_client.add("Session [DATE]: Completed [TASK]. Next task: [NEXT_TASK]. Phase: [N].")
# Save to Graphiti
graphiti_client.add_episode(name="session_[DATE]", episode_body="...", source_description="AI agent session")
```

---

## ⚡ QUICK DECISION RULES

| Question | Answer |
|----------|--------|
| Which LLM for answers? | Qwen3:4b via Ollama — always local, never cloud |
| Which embedding model? | paraphrase-multilingual-mpnet-base-v2 |
| Which vector DB? | Qdrant (self-hosted Docker) |
| Which RAG framework? | LlamaIndex |
| Which translation? | IndicTrans2 (online) / Opus-MT ONNX (offline) |
| Which STT? | faster-whisper-turbo (online) / whisper.cpp JNI (offline) |
| Which TTS? | Coqui XTTS-v2 (online) / Android TTS API (offline) |
| New Islamic source? | Ask developer for permission first — do NOT add automatically |
| Cloud LLM API? | NEVER — all inference is local on GTX 1650ti |
| Firebase? | NEVER — no Google telemetry |
| New feature without offline fallback? | REFUSE — implement all three tiers or ask how to |

## graphify

This project has a knowledge graph at graphify-out/ with god nodes, community structure, and cross-file relationships.

Rules:
- For codebase questions, first run `graphify query "<question>"` when graphify-out/graph.json exists. Use `graphify path "<A>" "<B>"` for relationships and `graphify explain "<concept>"` for focused concepts. These return a scoped subgraph, usually much smaller than GRAPH_REPORT.md or raw grep output.
- If graphify-out/wiki/index.md exists, use it for broad navigation instead of raw source browsing.
- Read graphify-out/GRAPH_REPORT.md only for broad architecture review or when query/path/explain do not surface enough context.
- After modifying code, run `graphify update .` to keep the graph current (AST-only, no API cost).

answerViewModel.currentAnswer.collectAsState()\n    val relatedVideos by answerViewModel.relatedVideos.collectAsState()\n    val isReadingAloud by answerViewModel.isReadingAloud.collectAsState()\n\n    // LocalContext is needed to start intents (like opening a web browser)\n    val context = LocalContext.current\n\n    Scaffold(\n        topBar = {\n            TopAppBar(\n                title = { longer than the screen.\n        // It only draws the content that is currently visible, saving memory.\n        LazyColumn(\n            modifier = Modifier\n                .fillMaxSize()\n                .padding(innerPadding)\n                .background(MaterialTheme.colorScheme.background),\n            contentPadding = PaddingValues(16.dp) // Add padding around all content inside the scroll\n        ) {\n            // We only show content if we actually have an answer to show\n            currentAnswer?.let { answer ->\n                \n                item {\n                   .background(QuranicBlue)\n                            .padding(horizontal = 12.dp, vertical = 6.dp)\n                    ) {\n                        Text(\n               }\n\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(16.dp))\n\n                    // The actual answer text. It should be large and readable.\n                    Text(\n                        text = answer.answerText,\n                        style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyLarge, // 18sp minimum\n                        color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onBackground,\n                        lineHeight = 28.sp // Extra line height for readability\n                    )\n\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(24.dp))\n\n                    // Clickable Source URL Row\n                    Row(verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically) {\n                        Text(\n                            text = \"మూలం / Source: \",\n                            style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium, // 16sp\n                            color = Color.Gray\n                        )\n                        \n                        // We build an \"Annotated String\" to make part of the text look like a clickable link\n                        val annotatedLinkString = buildAnnotatedString {\n                            withStyle(\n                                style = SpanStyle(\n                                    color = QuranicBlue,\n                                    textDecoration = TextDecoration.Underline,\n                                    fontSize = 16.sp\n                                )\n                            ) {\n                                append(\"View Original\")\n                            }\n                            // Attach the URL to this text segment\n                            addStringAnnotation(\n                                tag = \"URL\",\n                                annotation = answer.sourceUrl,\n                                start = 0,\n                                end = 13 // Length of \"View Original\"\n                            )\n                        }\n\n                        // ClickableText handles the tap event on the annotated string\n                        ClickableText(\n                            text = annotatedLinkString,\n                            onClick = { offset ->\n                                annotatedLinkString.getStringAnnotations(tag = \"URL\", start = offset, end = offset)\n                                    .firstOrNull()?.let { annotation ->\n                                        // Open the browser with the URL\n                                        val intent = Intent(Intent.ACTION_VIEW, Uri.parse(annotation.item))\n                                        context.startActivity(intent)\n                                    }\n                            }\n                        )\n                    }\n\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(16.dp))\n                    HorizontalDivider() // A thin line separating sections\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(16.dp))\n\n                    // Read Aloud Button - MUST be prominent and easily accessible\n                    Button(\n                        onClick = { answerViewModel.onReadAloudPressed() },\n                        modifier = Modifier\n                            .fillMaxWidth()\n                            .heightIn(min = 56.dp), // Large touch target\n                        // Change color if it is currently reading\n                        colors = ButtonDefaults.buttonColors(\n                            containerColor = if (isReadingAloud) Color.Gray else IslamicGreen\n                        )\n                    ) {\n                        Text(\n                            text = if (isReadingAloud) \"ఆపు / Stop Reading\" else \"🔊 చదివి వినిపించు / Read Aloud\",\n                            style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyLarge // 18sp\n                        )\n                    }\n\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(16.dp))\n                    HorizontalDivider()\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(16.dp))\n\n MaterialTheme.typography.titleLarge, // 22sp bold\n                        color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onBackground\n                    )\n\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(12.dp))\n                }\n\n                // Horizontal scrollable list for related videos\n                item {\n                    LazyRow(\n MicButton(\n    isRecording: Boolean,\n    onClick: () -> Unit\n) {\n    // Determine the color based on the recording state. \n    // We use the colors defined in our MaterialTheme.\n    val buttonColor = if (isRecording) {\n        MaterialTheme.colorScheme.error // ErrorRed (#B71C1C)\n    } else {\n        MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary // IslamicGreen (#2E7D32)\n    }\n\n    // Set up a pulsing animation when recording\n    // 'rememberInfiniteTransition' keeps an animation running repeatedly\n    val infiniteTransition = rememberInfiniteTransition(label = \"micPulse\")\n    val        animation = tween(durationMillis = 800),\n            // RepeatMode.Reverse makes it shrink back down smoothly\n            repeatMode = RepeatMode.Reverse\n        ),\n        label =    // It automatically handles the complex logic of opening the menu, positioning it, and closing it when tapped outside.\n    ExposedDropdownMenuBox(\n        expanded = expanded,\n        onExpandedChange = { expanded = it }, // Toggle the menu when tapped\n        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()\n    ) {\n        // The text field that the user actually sees before opening the menu.\n        OutlinedTextField(\n            value = displayLanguage,\n            onValueChange = {}, // Read-only, so we do nothing here\n            readOnly = true, // Prevent the keyboard from popping up\n            leadingIcon = { \n                Icon(\n                    imageVector = Icons.Default.Language, \n                    contentDescription = \"Language Icon\"\n                ) \n            },\n            trailingIcon = { \n                // Automatically draws a tiny down-arrow or up-arrow based on 'expanded' state\n                ExposedDropdownMenuDefaults.TrailingIcon(expanded = expanded) \n            },\n            modifier = Modifier\n                .menuAnchor() // Critical: tells the dropdown where to attach itself\n                .fillMaxWidth()\n                .heightIn(min = 56.dp), // Enforce minimum touch target height for accessibility\n            textStyle = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyLarge, // 18sp minimum for readability\n            colors = ExposedDropdownMenuDefaults.outlinedTextFieldColors()\n        )\n\n        // The actual pop-up menu containing the options\n        ExposedDropdownMenu(\n            expanded = expanded,\n            onDismissRequest = { expanded = false } // Close if user taps outside\n        ) {\n            // Loop through our language list and create an item for each one\n            languages.forEach { (languageKey, languageDisplay) ->\n                DropdownMenuItem(\n                    text = { \n                        Text(\n                            text = languageDisplay,\n                            style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyLarge // Large text for menu items too\n                        ) \n                    },\n                    onClick = {\n                        // When tapped, notify the parent and close the menu\n                        onLanguageSelected(languageKey)\n                        expanded = false\n                    },\n                    modifier = Modifier.heightIn(min = 48.dp) // Accessibility: min touch target inside menu\n                )\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// Preview to test the UI locally\n@Preview(showBackground = true)\n@Composable\nfun LanguageSelectorPreview() {\n    RushdulIlmTheme {\n        LanguageSelector(\n            selectedLanguage = \"Telugu\",\n            onLanguageSelected = {}\n        )\n    }\n}\n"

                                     context.startActivity(intent)\n                                    }\n                            }\n                        )\n                    }\n\n )\n                    ) {\n                        Text(\n                            text = if (isReadingAloud) \"ఆపు / Stop Reading\" else \"🔊 చదివి వినిపించు / Read Aloud\",\n                            style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyLarge // 18sp\n                        )\n                    }\n\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(16.dp))\n                    HorizontalDivider()\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(16.dp))\n\n                    // Related Videos Section Header\n                    Text(\n                        text = \"సంబంధిత వీడియోలు / Related Lectures\",\n                        style = MaterialTheme.typography.titleLarge, // 22sp bold\n                        color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onBackground\n                    )\n\n                    Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(12.dp))\n                }\n\n                // Horizontal scrollable list for related videos\n                item {\n                    LazyRow(\n                        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(16.dp), // Space between cards\n                        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth()\n                    ) {\n                        items(relatedVideos) { video ->\n                            AnswerVideoCard(video = video, onPlayClick = { answerViewModel.onVideoClicked(video) })\n                        }\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * A reusable component to display a single video suggestion.\n */\n@Composable\nfun AnswerVideoCard(video: RelatedVideo, onPlayClick: () -> Unit) {\n    Card(\n        modifier = Modifier\n            .width(280.dp) // Fixed width so they look like horizontal cards\n            .shadow(4.dp, RoundedCornerShape(8.dp)),\n        colors = CardDefaults.cardColors(containerColor = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.surface)\n    ) {\n        Column(modifier = Modifier.padding(12.dp)) {\n            // Scholar Name\n            Text(\n                text = video.scholarName,\n                style = MaterialTheme.typography.labelSmall, // 16sp\n                color = IslamicGreen\n            )\n            Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(4.dp))\n            // Video Title\n            Text(\n                text = video.title,\n                style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyLarge.copy(fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold), // 18sp\n                color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.onSurface,\n                maxLines = 2 // Prevent extremely long titles from breaking the layout\n            )\n            Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(4.dp))\n            \n            // Format duration from seconds to MM:SS\n            val minutes = video.durationSeconds / 60\n            val seconds = video.durationSeconds % 60\n            Text(\n                text = String.format(\"%02d:%02d\", minutes, seconds),\n                style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium, // 16sp\n                color = Color.Gray\n            )\n            \n            Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(8.dp))\n            \n            // Play Button\n            Button(\n                onClick = onPlayClick,\n                modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),\n                colors = ButtonDefaults.buttonColors(containerColor = QuranicBlue)\n            ) {\n                Text(\"▶ ప్లే చేయి / Play\", style = MaterialTheme.typography.bodyMedium)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n"
  }
}
```

androidx.compose.foundation.selection.selectableGroup\nimport androidx.compose.material.icons.Icons\nimport androidx.compose.material.icons.filled.ArrowBack\nimport androidx.compose.material.icons.filled.Download\nimport androidx.compose.material3.*\nimport androidx.compose.runtime.Composable\nimport androidx.compose.runtime.collectAsState\nimport androidx.compose.runtime.getValue\nimport androidx.compose.ui.Alignment\nimport androidx.compose.ui.Modifier\nimport androidx.compose.ui.graphics.Color\nimport androidx.compose.ui.semantics.Role\nimport androidx.compose.ui.text.font.FontWeight\nimport androidx.compose.ui.unit.dp\nimport androidx.compose.ui.unit.sp\nimport androidx.hilt.navigation.compose.hiltViewModel\nimport androidx.navigation.NavController\nimport androidx.compose.ui.res.stringResource\nimport com.rushdululilm.app.R\nimport com.rushdululilm.app.viewmodel.SettingsViewModel\n\n/**\n * SettingsScreen allows users to customize their experience and download offline data.\n * Analogy: Like a \"Settings\" menu on a phone where you change language or brightness.\n */\n@OptIn(ExperimentalMaterial3Api::class)\n@Composable\nfun SettingsScreen(\n    navController: NavController,\n    viewModel: SettingsViewModel = hiltViewModel() // Hilt injects our ViewModel automatically\n) {\n    // Observe state from the ViewModel\n    val selectedLanguage by viewModel.selectedLanguage.collectAsState()\n    val selectedMadhab by viewModel.selectedMadhab.collectAsState()\n    val isAutoPlayEnabled by viewModel.isAutoPlayEnabled.collectAsState()\n    val isLargeTextEnabled by viewModel.isLargeTextEnabled.collectAsState()\n\n    Scaffold(\n        topBar = {\n            TopAppBar(\n                title = { Text(stringResource(R.string.settings_label), fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold) },\n                navigationIcon = {\n                    IconButton(onClick = { navController.popBackStack() }) {\n                        Icon(imageVector = Icons.Default.ArrowBack, contentDescription = stringResource(R.string.icon_desc_back))\n                    }\n                }\n            )\n        }\n    ) { paddingValues ->\n        // LazyColumn is a vertical list that only draws what's visible on screen (efficient!)\n        LazyColumn(\n            modifier = Modifier\n                .fillMaxSize()\n                .padding(paddingValues)\n                .padding(16.dp),\n            verticalArrangement = Arrangement.spacedBy(24.dp) // Gap between sections\n        ) {\n            // --- SECTION 1: LANGUAGE SETTINGS ---\n            item {\n                SettingsSectionTitle(stringResource(R.string.language_selector_label))\n                val languages = listOf(\"Telugu\" to \"తెలుగు\", \"Urdu\" to \"اردو\", \"Hindi\" to \"हिंदी\", \"English\" to \"English\")\n                \n                Column(Modifier.selectableGroup()) {\n                    languages.forEach { (eng, local) ->\n                        SettingsRadioButton(\n                            label = \"$local ($eng)\",\n                            selected = selectedLanguage == eng,\n                            onClick = { viewModel.onLanguageSelected(eng) }\n                        )\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // --- SECTION 2: MADHAB PREFERENCE ---\n            item {\n                SettingsSectionTitle(stringResource(R.string.madhab_preference))\n                val madhabs = listOf(\"All Sources\", \"Neutral Only\", \"Hanafi (Deoband)\")\n                \n                Column(Modifier.selectableGroup()) {\n                    madhabs.forEach { madhab ->\n                        SettingsRadioButton(\n                            label = madhab,\n                            selected = selectedMadhab == madhab,\n                            onClick = { viewModel.onMadhabSelected(madhab) }\n                        )\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // --- SECTION 3: OFFLINE KNOWLEDGE DATABASE ---\n            item {\n                SettingsSectionTitle(stringResource(R.string.offline_knowledge_title))\n                \n                DownloadItem(\n                    name = \"IslamQA.info\",\n                    size = \"~500MB\",\n                    status = \"Not downloaded\",\n                    onDownload = { /* Placeholder */ }\n                )\n                \n                Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(12.dp))\n                \n                DownloadItem(\n                    name = \"Darul Ifta Deoband\",\n                    size = \"~200MB\",\n                    status = \"Downloaded\",\n                    onDownload = { /* Placeholder */ }\n                )\n            }\n\n            // --- SECTION 4: APP SETTINGS ---\n            item {\n                SettingsSectionTitle(\"App Settings / యాప్ సెట్టింగ్‌లు\")\n                \n                SettingsSwitch(\n                    label = \"Auto-play read aloud / ఆటో-ప్లే రీడ్ అలౌడ్\",\n                    checked = isAutoPlayEnabled,\n                    onCheckedChange = { viewModel.onAutoPlayToggled(it) }\n                )\n                \n                SettingsSwitch(\n                    label = \"Large text mode / పెద్ద వచన మోడ్\",\n                    checked = isLargeTextEnabled,\n                    onCheckedChange = { viewModel.onLargeTextToggled(it) }\n                )\n                \n                Spacer(modifier = Modifier.height(16.dp))\n                \n                Text(\n                    text = stringResource(R.string.app_version),\n                    fontSize = 14.sp,\n                    color = Color.Gray\n                )\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Reusable section title for Settings\n */\n@Composable\nfun SettingsSectionTitle(title: String) {\n    Text(\n        text = title,\n        fontSize = 20.sp,\n        fontWeight = FontWeight.ExtraBold,\n        color = MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary,\n        modifier = Modifier.padding(bottom = 8.dp)\n    )\n}\n\n/**\n * Reusable RadioButton row with a large touch target (48dp+)\n */\n@Composable\nfun SettingsRadioButton(label: String, selected: Boolean, onClick: () -> Unit) {\n    Row(\n        modifier = Modifier\n            .fillMaxWidth()\n            .height(56.dp) // High touch target for accessibility\n            .selectable(\n                selected = selected,\n                onClick = onClick,\n                role = Role.RadioButton\n            )\n            .padding(horizontal = 8.dp),\n        verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically\n    ) {\n        RadioButton(\n            selected = selected,\n            onClick = null // Handle click on the row for better UX\n        )\n        Spacer(modifier = Modifier.width(16.dp))\n        Text(text = label, fontSize = 18.sp)\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Reusable Switch row for binary settings\n */\n@Composable\nfun SettingsSwitch(label: String, checked: Boolean, onCheckedChange: (Boolean) -> Unit) {\n    Row(\n        modifier = Modifier\n            .fillMaxWidth()\n            .height(56.dp)\n            .padding(horizontal = 8.dp),\n        verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically,\n        horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.SpaceBetween\n    ) {\n        Text(text = label, fontSize = 18.sp, modifier = Modifier.weight(1f))\n        Switch(\n            checked = checked,\n            onCheckedChange = onCheckedChange\n        )\n    }\n}\n\n/**\n * Item for managing offline data downloads\n */\n@Composable\nfun DownloadItem(name: String, size: String, status: String, onDownload: () -> Unit) {\n    Card(\n        modifier = Modifier.fillMaxWidth(),\n        elevation = CardDefaults.cardElevation(defaultElevation = 2.dp)\n    ) {\n        Row(\n            modifier = Modifier\n                .padding(16.dp)\n                .fillMaxWidth(),\n            verticalAlignment = Alignment.CenterVertically,\n            horizontalArrangement = Arrangement.SpaceBetween\n        ) {\n            Column(modifier = Modifier.weight(1f)) {\n                Text(text = name, fontWeight = FontWeight.Bold, fontSize = 18.sp)\n                Text(text = \"$size | $status\", fontSize = 14.sp, color = Color.Gray)\n            }\n            Button(\n                onClick = onDownload,\n                colors = ButtonDefaults.buttonColors(\n                    containerColor = if (status == \"Downloaded\") Color(0xFF2E7D32) else MaterialTheme.colorScheme.primary\n                )\n            ) {\n                Icon(Icons.Default.Download, contentDescription = null)\n                Spacer(Modifier.width(4.dp))\n                Text(if (status == \"Downloaded\") \"Update\" else \"Download\")\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\nUpdate\" else \"Download\")\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n"
  }
}

androidx.navigation.compose.currentBackStackEntryAsState\nimport androidx.navigation.compose.rememberNavController\n\n/**\n * RushdulIlmNavGraph is the master UI container that handles switching between screens.\n * \n * Analogy: Think of this as a TV set. \n * - The 'NavHost' is the screen showing the current channel.\n * - The 'NavigationBar' at the bottom is the remote control buttons.\n * - Each 'composable' entry is a different TV channel (Screen).\n */\n@Composable\nfun RushdulIlmNavGraph() {\n    // 🎮 The NavController is our \"Remote Control\" - we use it to change screens\n    val navController = rememberNavController()\n\n    // 📱 Scaffold is a basic screen layout structure from Google's Material Design.\n    // It provides \"slots\" for things like a Top Bar, a Bottom Bar, and the Main Content.\n    Scaffold(\n        bottomBar = {\n            // 🏠 The Bottom Navigation Bar allows the user to switch between the 3 main areas\n            NavigationBar {\n                // We need to know which screen is currently visible to highlight the correct icon\n                val navBackStackEntry by navController.currentBackStackEntryAsState()\n                val currentDestination = navBackStackEntry?.destination\n\n                // 🔘 Home Button (Mic Screen)\n                NavigationBarItem(\n                    icon = { Icon(Icons.Default.Home, contentDescription = \"Home\") },\n                    label = { Text(\"Home\") },\n                    // Highlight this button if the current screen is HOME\n                    selected = currentDestination?.hierarchy?.any { it.route == Routes.HOME } == true,\n                    onClick = {\n                        // When clicked, tell the remote control to go to the Home route\n                        navController.navigate(Routes.HOME) {\n                            // Pop up to the start destination of the graph to\n                            // avoid building up a large stack of destinations\n                            popUpTo(navController.graph.findStartDestination().id) {\n                                saveState = true\n                            }\n                            // Avoid multiple copies of the same destination when\n                            // reselecting the same item\n                            launchSingleTop = true\n                            // Restore state when reselecting a previously selected item\n                            restoreState = true\n                        }\n                    }\n                )\n\n                // 🔘 Video Library Button\n                NavigationBarItem(\n                    icon = { Icon(Icons.Default.PlayArrow, contentDescription = \"Videos\") },\n                    label = { Text(\"Videos\") },\n                    selected = currentDestination?.hierarchy?.any { it.route == Routes.VIDEO_LIBRARY } == true,\n                    onClick = {\n                        navController.navigate(Routes.VIDEO_LIBRARY) {\n                            popUpTo(navController.graph.findStartDestination().id) {\n                                saveState = true\n                            }\n                            launchSingleTop = true\n                            restoreState = true\n                        }\n                    }\n                )\n\n                // 🔘 Settings Button\n                NavigationBarItem(\n                    icon = { Icon(Icons.Default.Settings, contentDescription = \"Settings\") },\n                    label = { Text(\"Settings\") },\n                    selected = currentDestination?.hierarchy?.any { it.route == Routes.SETTINGS } == true,\n                    onClick = {\n       }\n                            launchSingleTop = true\n                            restoreState = true\n                        }\n                    }\n                )\n            }\n        }\n    ) { innerPadding ->\n        // 🖼️ The NavHost is the \"Frame\" that swaps the actual screen content\n        // 'innerPadding' is provided by the Scaffold so our content doesn't hide behind the bottom bar\n        NavHost(\n            navController = navController,\n            startDestination = Routes.HOME, // The app starts on the Home screen\n            modifier = Modifier.padding(innerPadding) // Apply the padding from the Scaffold\n        ) {\n            // 📍 Register the Home Screen route\n            composable(Routes.HOME) {\n                HomeScreen(navController)\n            }\n\n            // 📍 Register the Answer Screen route\n            // Note: This screen is not in the bottom bar, it is opened from Home\n            composable(Routes.ANSWER) {\n                AnswerScreen(navController)\n            }\n\n            // 📍 Register the Video Library route\n            composable(Routes.VIDEO_LIBRARY) {\n                VideoLibraryScreen(navController)\n            }\n\n            // 📍 Register the Settings Screen route\n            composable(Routes.SETTINGS) {\n                SettingsScreen(navController)\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n"

navController = rememberNavController()\n\n    // 📱 Scaffold is a basic screen layout structure from Google's Material Design.\n    // It provides \"slots\" for things like a Top Bar, a Bottom Bar, and the Main Content.\n    Scaffold(\n        bottomBar = {\n            // 🏠 The Bottom Navigation Bar allows the user to switch between the 3 main areas\n            NavigationBar {\n                // We need to know which screen is currently visible to highlight the correct icon\n                val navBackStackEntry by navController.currentBackStackEntryAsState()\n                val currentDestination = navBackStackEntry?.destination\n\n                // 🔘 Home Button (Mic Screen)\n                NavigationBarItem(\n                    icon = { Icon(Icons.Default.Home, contentDescription = \"Home\") },\n                    label = { Text(\"Home\") },\n                    // Highlight this button if the current screen is HOME\n                    selected = currentDestination?.hierarchy?.any { it.route == Routes.HOME } == true,\n                    onClick = {\n                        // When clicked, tell the remote control to go to the Home route\n                        navController.navigate(Routes.HOME) {\n                            // Pop up to the start destination of the graph to\n                            // avoid building up a large stack of destinations\n                            popUpTo(navController.graph.findStartDestination().id) {\n                                saveState = true\n                            }\n                            // Avoid multiple copies of the same destination when\n                            // reselecting the same item\n                            launchSingleTop = true\n                            // Restore state when reselecting a previously selected item\n                            restoreState = true\n                        }\n                    }\n                )\n\n content doesn't hide behind the bottom bar\n        NavHost(\n            navController = navController,\n            startDestination = Routes.HOME, // The app starts on the Home screen\n            modifier = Modifier.padding(innerPadding) // Apply the padding from the Scaffold\n        ) {\n            // 📍 Register the Home Screen route\n            composable(Routes.HOME) {\n                HomeScreen(navController)\n            }\n\n            // 📍 Register the Answer Screen route\n            // Note: This screen is not in the bottom bar, it is opened from Home\n ### Concept Explanation: Android String Resources
**What it is:** Android provides a built-in way to organize text used in the UI outside of the actual code files by using a specific file named `strings.xml`.
**Analogy:** Think of `strings.xml` as a dictionary or a lookup table. Instead of writing the actual word "Apple" inside a book you're writing, you write `Word #1`. When someone reads the book in English, `Word #1` translates to "Apple". When they read it in Telugu, the Telugu dictionary tells them it's "ఆపిల్".
**Why it matters:** Using `stringResource(...)` allows Android to automatically switch the text depending on the device's selected language, ensuring we avoid hardcoded values that are difficult to update and translate later.
